   636	      #   - GPG signature present + verifies against owner.asc
   637	      #
   638	      # continue-on-error: ONLY when CEO_PAIR_RAIL_VERDICT_OPTIONAL=1 env
   639	      # explicitly set (e.g. legacy rc tags pre-verdict-rollout). Default is
   640	      # hard-block on any validator failure.
   641	      - name: Validate pair-rail verdict (PLAN-081 Phase 6-bis step 15)
   642	        env:
   643	          # Codex iter-8 P1 fix: source the env var from a repository
   644	          # variable so the `continue-on-error` expression has something
   645	          # to evaluate against. Owner sets via `gh variable set
   646	          # CEO_PAIR_RAIL_VERDICT_OPTIONAL --body 1` for transition mode
   647	          # (e.g. legacy v1.16.0-era verdicts shipping only commit_sha:);
   648	          # unset / 0 = hard-block (default).
   649	          CEO_PAIR_RAIL_VERDICT_OPTIONAL: ${{ vars.CEO_PAIR_RAIL_VERDICT_OPTIONAL || '0' }}
   650	        continue-on-error: ${{ vars.CEO_PAIR_RAIL_VERDICT_OPTIONAL == '1' }}
   651	        run: |
   652	          set -euo pipefail
   653	          VERDICT_FILE=".claude/governance/pair-rail-verdict-${GITHUB_REF_NAME}.md"
   654	          if [ ! -f "$VERDICT_FILE" ]; then
   655	            if [ "${CEO_PAIR_RAIL_VERDICT_OPTIONAL:-0}" = "1" ]; then
   656	              echo "::notice::no verdict file at $VERDICT_FILE; CEO_PAIR_RAIL_VERDICT_OPTIONAL=1 → skipping"
   657	              exit 0
   658	            fi
   659	            echo "::error::verdict file missing at $VERDICT_FILE — step 15 blocks release"
   660	            exit 1
   661	          fi
   662	          # S104 redesign: resolve PARENT_SHA = parent of the verdict-file
   663	          # commit. The tag commit (${GITHUB_SHA}) is what we're releasing,
   664	          # and the verdict file at $VERDICT_FILE either:
   665	          #   (a) was committed in the tag commit itself → parent = ${GITHUB_SHA}^
   666	          #   (b) was committed earlier (multi-commit prep) → parent = git log of file
   667	          # We use (b)'s general form: find the commit that introduced the
   668	          # current verdict file, then take its parent. This handles both
   669	          # single-commit-with-verdict and multi-commit-prep flows.
   670	          VERDICT_FILE_COMMIT=$(git log -n1 --format=%H -- "$VERDICT_FILE")
   671	          if [ -z "$VERDICT_FILE_COMMIT" ]; then
   672	            echo "::error::cannot resolve commit for $VERDICT_FILE — step 15 fails"
   673	            exit 1
   674	          fi
   675	          PARENT_SHA=$(git rev-parse "${VERDICT_FILE_COMMIT}^" 2>/dev/null || echo "")
   676	          if [ -z "$PARENT_SHA" ]; then
   677	            echo "::error::cannot resolve parent of $VERDICT_FILE_COMMIT — step 15 fails"
   678	            exit 1
   679	          fi
   680	          echo "::notice::S104 bind: VERDICT_FILE_COMMIT=$VERDICT_FILE_COMMIT, PARENT_SHA=$PARENT_SHA"
   681	          # When transition mode is on, allow parent_sha mismatch (skip bind)
   682	          # by passing empty string. Default is hard-bind on PARENT_SHA.
   683	          PARENT_SHA_ARG="$PARENT_SHA"
   684	          if [ "${CEO_PAIR_RAIL_VERDICT_OPTIONAL:-0}" = "1" ]; then
   685	            PARENT_SHA_ARG=""
   686	          fi
   687	          python3 .github/scripts/validate-pair-rail-verdict.py \
   688	            --verdict-file "$VERDICT_FILE" \
   689	            --parent-sha "$PARENT_SHA_ARG" \
   690	            --release-tag "${GITHUB_REF_NAME}" \
   691	            --max-age-hours 24 \
   692	            --recompute-inputs-hash \
   693	            --codex-cli-pin-file .claude/governance/codex-cli-pin.txt \
   694	            --codex-cli-binary-sha256-file .claude/governance/codex-cli-binary-sha256.txt \
   695	            --inputs-hash-paths-file .claude/governance/pair-rail-inputs-hash-manifest.txt

   118	      # F5 — RC-hold / staleness waiver SUNSET assertion.
   119	      #
   120	      # The pre-GA waivers in .claude/governance/governance-waivers.yaml
   121	      # are honest ONLY while the project is pre-GA (adopter_count=0).
   122	      # Every existing rc_hold/workflow_staleness entry is a 1.x version
   123	      # carrying "Pre-GA ... adopter_count=0". To stop that 100%-waiver
   124	      # escape from silently following the project into GA, this step
   125	      # FAILS the release the moment any waiver `version` parses >= the
   126	      # configured FIRST_GA floor. The floor is the first version at which
   127	      # the framework intends to claim GA / publish to adopters; per
   128	      # ADR-073 the next major (v2.0.0) is the documented GA/breaking
   129	      # boundary, so 2.0.0 is the mechanical sunset. After the first real
   130	      # adopter ships, lower FIRST_GA (or empty the waiver lists) so the
   131	      # ADR-007 RC-hold + 14-day staleness gates resume real enforcement.
   132	      #
   133	      # Today (max waiver 1.0.0 < 2.0.0) this passes; it is a tripwire,
   134	      # not a behavior change for the current pre-GA train.
   135	      #
   136	      # `-rc.N` pre-release suffixes are stripped before comparison: RC
   137	      # tags forensically short-circuit the hold gate (see below), so an
   138	      # rc.* waiver is never an enforcement bypass on its own.
   139	      # -----------------------------------------------------------------
   140	      - name: Assert no waiver has reached the GA sunset floor
   141	        env:
   142	          # First version at which pre-GA waivers are no longer honest.
   143	          # Bump DOWN (or empty the waiver lists) once an adopter ships.
   144	          FIRST_GA: "2.0.0"
   145	        run: |
   146	          set -euo pipefail
   147	          WAIVER_FILE=".claude/governance/governance-waivers.yaml"
   148	          if [[ ! -f "$WAIVER_FILE" ]]; then
   149	            echo "OK: no waiver file present — nothing to sunset"
   150	            exit 0
   151	          fi
   152	
   153	          # Extract every `version:` value from BOTH waiver sections using
   154	          # the same flag-based section parser the file documents (a range
   155	          # pattern collapses because the start/end regex overlap), strip
   156	          # any -rc.* suffix, then sort -V -u. Iterated via a while-read
   157	          # loop (portable: no mapfile / bash-4 dependency).
   158	          FAILED=0
   159	          COUNT=0
   160	          while IFS= read -r v; do
   161	            [[ -z "$v" ]] && continue
   162	            COUNT=$((COUNT + 1))
   163	            # v >= FIRST_GA  <=>  the smaller of {v, FIRST_GA} under
   164	            # version-sort is FIRST_GA. (Equal floor counts as reached.)
   165	            LOWER="$(printf '%s\n%s\n' "$v" "$FIRST_GA" | sort -V | head -1)"
   166	            if [[ "$v" == "$FIRST_GA" || "$LOWER" == "$FIRST_GA" ]]; then
   167	              echo "::error::Waiver version $v has reached the GA sunset floor (FIRST_GA=$FIRST_GA)"
   168	              echo "::error::Pre-GA RC-hold/staleness waivers are dishonest at or past GA."
   169	              echo "::error::Remove the $v waiver entry (and resume ADR-007 enforcement) or lower FIRST_GA only with a real adopter."
   170	              FAILED=1
   171	            fi
   172	          done < <(
   173	            {
   174	              awk '/^rc_hold:/{f=1; next} f && /^[a-z_]+:/{f=0} f' "$WAIVER_FILE"
   175	              awk '/^workflow_staleness:/{f=1; next} f && /^[a-z_]+:/{f=0} f' "$WAIVER_FILE"
   176	            } \
   177	              | grep -oE '^[[:space:]]*-[[:space:]]*version:[[:space:]]*[0-9][0-9A-Za-z.+-]*' \
   178	              | grep -oE '[0-9][0-9A-Za-z.+-]*$' \
   179	              | sed -E 's/-rc\.[0-9.]+$//' \
   180	              | sort -V -u
   181	          )
   182	
   183	          if [[ "$COUNT" -eq 0 ]]; then
   184	            echo "OK: waiver file has no version entries to sunset"
   185	            exit 0
   186	          fi
   187	          if [[ "$FAILED" -ne 0 ]]; then
   188	            exit 1
   189	          fi
   190	          echo "OK: all $COUNT waiver versions are pre-GA (< FIRST_GA=$FIRST_GA)"
   191	
   192	      # -----------------------------------------------------------------
   193	      # PLAN-112-FOLLOWUP-canonical-doc-refresh-gate — canonical doc freshness.
   194	      #
   195	      # Fails the release when an in-scope canonical doc's machine-readable
   196	      # `<!-- last-reviewed: DATE vX.Y.Z -->` stamp is more MINOR releases
   197	      # behind VERSION than its tier allows (security docs N=1; general N=3).
   198	      # Missing/malformed stamp fails-CLOSED. Closes F-D4.
   199	      #
   200	      # Emergency bypass: the checker self-reads an Owner-signed
   201	      # `doc_freshness:` entry (matching this release version) in
   202	      # `.claude/governance/governance-waivers.yaml` and, when present,
   203	      # passes WITH a surfaced ::warning (never a silent skip).
   204	      # -----------------------------------------------------------------
   205	      - name: Canonical doc freshness gate
   206	        run: |
   207	          set -euo pipefail
   208	          python3 .claude/scripts/check-canonical-doc-freshness.py
   209	
   210	      # -----------------------------------------------------------------
   211	      # PLAN-013 Phase 0 item 0.3 — mandatory RC-to-GA hold enforcement.
   212	      # AMENDED 2026-05-03 per ADR-103: 7-day calendar gate REDUCED to
   213	      # 24h Codex re-pass mechanical window per ADR-095 §gate-#6.
   214	      #
   215	      # Debate Round 1 consensus §S3 HIGH (DevOps): "7-day RC hold is
   216	      # policy not mechanism. Policy without mechanism is hope."
   217	      #
   218	      # Rule: a GA tag `v1.x.y` MAY only ship after its corresponding
   219	      # RC tag `v1.x.y-rc.N` has existed for ≥24 hours. The 24h window
   220	      # is mechanical: bounds the maximum Codex external re-pass
   221	      # turnaround (anti same-LLM bias per ADR-095 §gate-#6). NOT a
   222	      # "settle period" — vibecoder-only thesis (ADR-096) means no
   223	      # external adopter pressure for calendar buffers.
   224	      #
   225	      # Mechanism:
   226	      #   1. If tag contains `-rc.` → skip check (RC tags always pass)
   227	      #   2. Else find most recent `v<VERSION>-rc.*` tag (by creator date)
   228	      #   3. If none exists → fail (mandatory RC before GA)
   229	      #   4. Else compute delta; reject if < 24h (86400 seconds)
   230	      # -----------------------------------------------------------------
   231	      - name: Assert 24h Codex re-pass window (GA tags only, waiver-aware)
   232	        run: |
   233	          set -euo pipefail
   234	          TAG="${GITHUB_REF_NAME}"
   235	          VERSION="${TAG#v}"
   236	
   237	          # RC tags short-circuit — they are always permitted.
   238	          if [[ "$TAG" == *-rc.* ]]; then
   239	            echo "::notice::$TAG is an RC tag — skipping 24h hold check"
   240	            exit 0
   241	          fi
   242	
   243	          # Pre-GA waiver check (PLAN-051 round-19, ADR-007 amendment).
   244	          # During initial framework development with adopter_count=0,
   245	          # the RC-hold window can be waived per Owner authorization
   246	          # recorded in .claude/governance/rc-hold-waivers.yaml. The
   247	          # waiver is additive: post-first-adopter, the file is expected
   248	          # to be empty and ADR-007 default resumes. Each waiver entry
   249	          # cites Owner directive + round-NN sentinel commit.
   250	          WAIVER_FILE=".claude/governance/governance-waivers.yaml"
   251	          if [[ -f "$WAIVER_FILE" ]]; then
   252	            if awk '/^rc_hold:/{f=1; next} f && /^[a-z_]+:/{f=0} f' "$WAIVER_FILE" | grep -qE "^[[:space:]]*-[[:space:]]*version:[[:space:]]*${VERSION}[[:space:]]*$"; then
   253	              echo "::notice::$TAG has a pre-GA RC-hold waiver in $WAIVER_FILE — skipping hold check"
   254	              exit 0
   255	            fi
   256	          fi
   257	
   258	          # Find the most-recent RC tag for this version, by creator date.
   259	          # `git tag -l --sort=-creatordate` handles both lightweight and
   260	          # annotated tags uniformly via the dereferenced date.
   261	          LAST_RC=$(git tag -l --sort=-creatordate "v${VERSION}-rc.*" | head -1)
   262	
   263	          if [[ -z "$LAST_RC" ]]; then
   264	            echo "::error::GA tag $TAG has no prior v${VERSION}-rc.* tag"
   265	            echo "::error::Mandatory RC-hold requires a prior RC tag"
   266	            echo "::error::Cut v${VERSION}-rc.1 first; wait 24h (Codex re-pass turnaround); then cut $TAG"
   267	            exit 1
   268	          fi
   269	
   270	          # Creator-date gives a unix-epoch timestamp for both
   271	          # annotated (tagger date) and lightweight (committer date) tags.
   272	          RC_TS=$(git tag -l --format='%(creatordate:unix)' "$LAST_RC")
   273	          GA_TS=$(git tag -l --format='%(creatordate:unix)' "$TAG")
   274	
   275	          if [[ -z "$RC_TS" || -z "$GA_TS" ]]; then
   276	            echo "::error::Could not read creator-date for $LAST_RC or $TAG"
   277	            exit 1
   278	          fi
   279	
   280	          DELTA=$((GA_TS - RC_TS))
   281	          ONE_DAY=$((1 * 86400))
   282	          HOURS=$((DELTA / 3600))
   283	
   284	          if [[ "$DELTA" -lt "$ONE_DAY" ]]; then
   285	            echo "::error::GA tag $TAG is only $HOURS hours after $LAST_RC"
   286	            echo "::error::Mandatory 24h Codex re-pass window not met (delta=${DELTA}s < 86400s)"
   287	            echo "::error::Wait $((24 - HOURS)) more hours OR run Codex re-pass synchronously and add waiver"
   288	            exit 1
   289	          fi
   290	
   291	          echo "OK: $TAG is $HOURS hours after $LAST_RC (≥24h Codex re-pass window per ADR-103)"
   292	
   293	      - name: Assert CHANGELOG entry exists
   294	        run: |
   295	          set -euo pipefail
   296	          TAG="${GITHUB_REF_NAME}"
   297	          VERSION="${TAG#v}"
   298	          # PLAN-153 Wave B item 5 (c) — same RC normalization as the
   299	          # "Assert VERSION matches tag" step above: RC tags never get
   300	          # their own CHANGELOG section; an RC for X.Y.Z validates
   301	          # against the GA `## [X.Y.Z]` section (which exists at RC-cut
   302	          # time because the VERSION bump + CHANGELOG entry land before
   303	          # the RC is tagged). Without this strip the fixed VERSION gate
   304	          # would just move the RC red run one step later.
   305	          VERSION="${VERSION%-rc.[0-9]*}"
   306	          if ! grep -qE "^## \[${VERSION}\]" CHANGELOG.md; then
   307	            echo "::error::CHANGELOG.md has no '## [${VERSION}]' section"
   308	            exit 1
   309	          fi
   310	          echo "OK: CHANGELOG has entry for [$VERSION]"

exec

   179	        # last line. At publish time, compute sha256 of the script body
   180	        # (all lines EXCEPT the last) and substitute the placeholder with
   181	        # the real hex. The script's own self-verify logic reads the same
   182	        # last-line pattern, so downstream adopters running
   183	        # `bash install.sh ...` trigger a rc=5 fail-CLOSED if the script
   184	        # is modified in transit.

   191	            echo "::error::$FILE trailer not at expected placeholder state"
   192	            echo "got: $TRAILER_LINE"
   193	            exit 1
   194	          fi
   195	          # Compute sha of everything EXCEPT the last line.
   196	          HASH=$(awk 'NR==FNR{n++; next} FNR < n' "$FILE" "$FILE" | sha256sum | awk '{print $1}')
   197	          # In-place substitute ONLY the last line.
   198	          awk -v hash="$HASH" '
   199	            NR == FNR { total = NR; next }
   200	            FNR == total { print "# CEO-INSTALL-SHA256: " hash; next }
   201	            { print }
   202	          ' "$FILE" "$FILE" > "$FILE.new"
   203	          mv "$FILE.new" "$FILE"

   206	          # the script without args (hits _verify_self_sha, then usage).

   239	      # previously successful publish, or a re-run after a post-publish
   240	      # step failed), the Publish step is skipped and the job succeeds
   241	      # as a documented no-op instead of going red on EPUBLISHCONFLICT.
   242	      #
   243	      # Detection is deliberately conservative: "published" ONLY when
   244	      # `npm view <name>@<version> version` exits 0 AND prints exactly
   245	      # the version (npm has historically flip-flopped between
   246	      # rc!=0/E404 and rc=0/empty-stdout for a missing version of an
   247	      # existing package — both shapes are treated as not-published).
   248	      # Any registry/network error therefore falls through to the
   249	      # publish attempt, which preserves today's behavior (npm itself
   250	      # fails closed on a true conflict). No auth needed: the package
   251	      # is public and `npm view` is an unauthenticated read.
   252	      # -----------------------------------------------------------------
   253	      - name: Check registry for already-published version
   254	        id: already_published
   255	        working-directory: npm
   256	        run: |
   257	          set -euo pipefail
   258	          PKG_NAME=$(node -p "require('./package.json').name")
   259	          PKG_VERSION=$(node -p "require('./package.json').version")
   260	          set +e
   261	          SEEN=$(npm view "${PKG_NAME}@${PKG_VERSION}" version 2>/dev/null)
   262	          RC=$?
   263	          set -e
   264	          if [[ "$RC" -eq 0 && "$SEEN" == "$PKG_VERSION" ]]; then
   265	            echo "published=true" >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
   266	            echo "::notice::${PKG_NAME}@${PKG_VERSION} already exists in the registry — publish will be skipped (idempotent re-run, succeed-as-noop)"
   267	          else
   268	            echo "published=false" >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
   269	            echo "OK: ${PKG_NAME}@${PKG_VERSION} not in registry (rc=$RC) — proceeding to publish"
   270	          fi
   271	
   272	      - name: Publish (Trusted Publishing — OIDC)
   273	        if: steps.already_published.outputs.published != 'true'
   274	        working-directory: npm
   275	        # PLAN-158 W1: NO long-lived token — npm >=11.5.1 detects the
   276	        # GitHub Actions OIDC context and mints a short-lived credential
   277	        # against the npmjs trusted-publisher registration (repo
   278	        # Canhada-Labs/ceo-orchestration, workflow npm-publish.yml,
   279	        # environment production-npm). --provenance keeps working (same
   280	        # OIDC JWT feeds Sigstore).
   281	        #
   282	        # ROLLBACK (token fallback) — kept dormant BY DESIGN, do not
   283	        # inline-enable: apply
   284	        # .claude/plans/PLAN-158/staged/wave1/rollback-oidc-to-token.patch
   285	        # (restores the `env: NODE_AUTH_TOKEN` block below), regenerate a

   759	      # PLAN-153 Wave B item 5 (b) — idempotent release creation
   760	      # (`gh release view || gh release create`). A re-run of this job
   761	      # (workflow re-run, transient asset-upload failure) must not fail
   762	      # on an existing release: if the release already exists we
   763	      # re-sync the assets with `--clobber` and succeed-as-noop —
   764	      # covering the partial-failure case where `gh release create`
   765	      # made the release but died mid-asset-upload.
   766	      # RC tags (which reach this job since the RC-aware VERSION gate
   767	      # fix) are marked --prerelease so they never show as "Latest".
   768	      # NOTE: bash arrays are fine here — this runs on ubuntu-latest
   769	      # (bash 5); the bash-3.2 house rule applies to adopter-machine
   770	      # scripts (install.sh), and release.yml already uses arrays in
   771	      # the weekly-workflow gate (WORKFLOWS=(...)).
   772	      # -----------------------------------------------------------------
   773	      - name: Create GitHub Release with assets (idempotent)
   774	        env:
   775	          GH_TOKEN: ${{ github.token }}
   776	        run: |
   777	          set -euo pipefail
   778	          TAG="${GITHUB_REF_NAME}"
   779	          if gh release view "$TAG" >/dev/null 2>&1; then
   780	            echo "::notice::release $TAG already exists — idempotent re-run; re-syncing assets with --clobber instead of create"
   781	            gh release upload "$TAG" --clobber install.sh.sha256 sbom.cyclonedx.json
   782	            exit 0
   783	          fi
   784	          CREATE_ARGS=(--verify-tag --title "$TAG" --notes-file release-notes.md)
   785	          if [[ "$TAG" == *-rc.* ]]; then
   786	            CREATE_ARGS+=(--prerelease)
   787	          fi

 succeeded in 0ms:
    45	
    46	## Versioning
    47	
    48	The shim's version follows the framework's `VERSION` file 1:1. They
    49	are bumped together. There is no separate semver track for the npm
    50	package; if `VERSION=1.2.3`, the npm package is `1.2.3`.
    51	
    52	## Publishing
    53	
    54	`ceo-orchestration` is published from CI on tag push (`v*`) via
    55	`.github/workflows/npm-publish.yml`. Manual `npm publish` is not
    56	used; tags are the only entry point. RC tags (`-rc.*`) are excluded
    57	at the job level; only GA tags publish.
    58	
    59	Registry authentication is npm **Trusted Publishing** (OIDC): the
    60	per-run GitHub OIDC JWT (`id-token: write`) is exchanged by npm CLI
    61	>=11.5.1 (upgraded in-job — Node 20 bundles npm 10.x) for a
    62	short-lived publish credential scoped to the registered trusted
    63	publisher (repo `Canhada-Labs/ceo-orchestration`, workflow
    64	`npm-publish.yml`, environment `production-npm` — an Owner
    65	web-console registration on npmjs.com), still gated behind the
    66	`production-npm` GitHub environment (manual approval before any
    67	publish step). The same JWT feeds the Sigstore `--provenance`
    68	attestation. No long-lived registry token is used: the former
    69	`NPM_TOKEN` granular token is revoked once the first OIDC GA publish
    70	succeeds (PLAN-158 Wave 1, successor of PLAN-152 §Deferred
    71	`backlog-oidc`; until that proof, a rollback to token auth is
    72	pre-staged at
    73	`.claude/plans/PLAN-158/staged/wave1/rollback-oidc-to-token.patch`).
    74	
    75	The publish workflow:
    76	1. Verifies `npm/package.json` `version` matches `VERSION`.
    77	2. Verifies the bundle includes `scripts/install.sh`.
    78	3. Asserts `dependencies` is empty.
    79	4. Publishes with `--provenance` (npm provenance via Sigstore).
    80	
    81	## Exit codes
    82	
    83	| Code | Meaning |
    84	|---|---|
    85	| 0..N | Whatever `install.sh` returned (passthrough) |
    86	| 1 | Spawn killed by signal (no exit code captured) |
    87	| 2 | `install.sh` missing from bundle (packaging bug, not user error) |
    88	
    89	## Deprecation
    90	
    91	No flags or behaviors deprecated in v1.0.0-rc.1.
    92	
    93	Future deprecation requires:
    94	- `deprecated_in: "1.X.0"` in this file
    95	- `removed_in: "2.0.0"` in this file
    96	- stdout warning when the deprecated behavior is observed
    97	- 90-day window before removal
    98	
    99	## Cross-reference
   100	
   101	- `SPEC/v1/install-cli.md` — the install.sh flag contract this shim
   102	  forwards to.
   103	- `.github/workflows/smoke-install.yml` — pre-merge gate that runs
   104	  `bash install.sh` AND (when the npm/ subtree changes) checks the
   105	  npm shim's contract.
   106	- ADR-012 — cross-adapter golden fixtures + OIDC trusted-publisher
   107	  rationale (target end-state; not yet configured — see §Publishing).
   108	
   109	## Version history
   110	
   111	| SPEC version | Changes |
   112	|---|---|
   113	| 1.0.0-rc.1 | Initial formal contract; pass-through shim with zero deps |
   114	| 1.0.1-rc.1 | §Publishing corrected: publish auth is a repo-scoped npm granular token + Sigstore `--provenance` attestation; the "OIDC trusted publisher" claim removed (never configured — same false-claim class as the npm-publish.yml header fixed by PLAN-152 tarball-01). Trusted Publishing tracked for v1.0.2 (PLAN-152 §Deferred `backlog-oidc`). Documentation correction only; no contract or behavioral change. |

Documentation-of-mechanism change; no shim contract or behavioral change (PLAN-158 Wave 1). |

     1	# Changelog
     2	
     3	All notable changes to **ceo-orchestration** are documented in this file.
     4	
     5	The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.1.0/),
     6	and this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html).
     7	
     8	> **Scope.** This log records *user-visible* changes — new skills, hooks, slash
     9	> commands, schema/contract changes, and behavior an adopter would notice after
    10	> installing or upgrading the framework. Internal refactors, test-only churn, and
    11	> release-engineering bookkeeping are omitted. Counts cited below (as of
    12	> v1.1.0: 166 skills, 26 slash commands, 177 ADRs, 68 `_lib` modules) are
    13	> reproducible from the repository via
    14	> `bash .claude/scripts/local/verify-counts.sh`.
    15	
    16	---
    17	
    18	## [1.1.0] - 2026-07-13
    19	
    20	Feature release (PLAN-153/154/155/156): two new host harnesses (Codex CLI
    21	and Grok Build run the same enforcement hooks), a cross-vendor audit
    22	council, a gated learning loop, and a skill-catalog uplift 151 → 166. As
    23	always: governance and auditability — no speed claim.
    24	
    25	### Added — multi-harness (PLAN-155, PLAN-156)
    26	- **`--harness codex`** (PLAN-155, ADR-161): the installer emits a Codex
    27	  bundle (`.codex/hooks.json`, `.codex/rules/ceo.rules`, operator
    28	  `AGENTS.md`) that runs the **same** hooks under `CEO_HOOK_ADAPTER=codex`.
    29	  Per-rail truth (verified against codex-cli 0.139.0): canonical-edit,
    30	  bash-safety, plan-lifecycle, kernel-deny, config, and kill-switch are
    31	  ENFORCED at edit time; audit chain ENFORCED but completeness-bounded;
    32	  pair-rail inverted (Codex operates, `claude -p` reviews) and PARTIAL;
    33	  spawn governance ADVISORY. Installer ends with an
    34	  `ARMED / NOT-ARMED-(untrusted) / BROKEN` arming check.
    35	- **`--harness grok`** (PLAN-156, ADR-162): single-surface install — Grok
    36	  Build reads the shipped `.claude/settings.json` directly (no second
    37	  bundle; arming both surfaces would double-fire every hook). Prevention
    38	  rails ENFORCED via grok's `pre_tool_use`; pair-rail is Stop-passive, so
    39	  a **git pre-push review gate is the teeth**. Verified against grok
    40	  0.2.93 (exact pin). Emits `AGENTS.md` + `.grok/*.example` config.
    41	- New docs: [`docs/adapters.md`](docs/adapters.md) +
    42	  [`docs/provider_capability_matrix.md`](docs/provider_capability_matrix.md)
    43	  (per-rail, per-harness enforcement matrix — what is actually enforced
    44	  vs advisory under each harness).
    45	- Audit-chain action registry extended for both harnesses (314 → 319
    46	  registered actions, tamper-mirror coverage included).
    47	- codex-cli version pin bumped to `<0.145.0` (GPT-5.6 line) in
    48	  `codex-cli-pin.txt`; release gate hard-blocks verdicts from unpinned
    49	  codex binaries.
    50	
    51	### Added — cross-vendor audit council (PLAN-156)
    52	- **`/council <scope>`** — read-only, three-vendor audit (Claude in-harness
    53	  agents + Codex `exec --sandbox read-only` + Grok `-p --sandbox council`)
    54	  with vendor-attributed verdicts, adversarial re-verification, and
    55	  explicit fail-loud quorum degradation (an unavailable lane reports
    56	  STATUS: unavailable, never a silent substitution). Every external-lane
    57	  prompt passes the ADR-114 egress redactor; ADVISORY evidence only;
    58	  operator/local only — never CI.
    59	
    60	### Added — gated learning loop (PLAN-154)
    61	- Hooks accrue **lesson candidates** from live sessions; nothing renders
    62	  or persists as advice until explicitly approved: **`/lesson-review`**
    63	  (approve / reject / undo, HMAC-recorded), **`/lesson-evolve`** (cluster
    64	  approved lessons into SP-NNN skill-patch drafts for the existing
    65	  /skill-review ceremony), and an opt-in boot surface
    66	  (`CEO_LEARNING_BOOT_LESSONS=1`) that renders ≤3 verified one-liners as
    67	  fenced untrusted data — verify-before-render against the HMAC chain,
    68	  fail-closed drops, count-only integrity notes. Default OFF
    69	  (`CEO_SOTA_DISABLE=1` master kill precedence).
    70	
    71	### Added — skill catalog + commands (PLAN-153)
    72	- Skill catalog **151 → 166**: 15 imported domain skills land through a
    73	  new import gate with a NOTICE provenance ledger; 20+ SP-NNN adaptation
    74	  patches promoted shadow → live through the new **`/skill-review`**
    75	  ceremony (staged shadow-soak, Owner-waivable).
    76	- New commands: **`/skill-health`** (per-skill telemetry from the HMAC
    77	  audit log — invocations, failure-proxy clusters, dead-skill flagging)
    78	  and **`/context-budget`** (static context-overhead audit of the skill
    79	  catalog + governance surface).
    80	- `COMMAND→SKILL→HOOK` map (`docs/COMMAND-SKILL-HOOK-MAP.md`) with a
    81	  validate.yml drift gate — regenerate via
    82	  `.claude/scripts/gen-command-skill-hook-map.py --write`.
    83	
    84	### Added — security gates (PLAN-153 Wave E)
    85	- Harness-config gate (tamper tripwires over `settings.json` hook
    86	  registrations), citation gate, spawn prompt-defense template, deny
    87	  baseline, and supply-chain watch — all wired into `/ceo-boot` +
    88	  validate.yml.
    89	
    90	### Added — installer / release lifecycle (PLAN-153 Wave B)
    91	- `doctor.sh` + repair mode, install-state manifest + replay,
    92	  install-profiles manifest, deterministic plugin-manifest regeneration
    93	  (`build-plugin.py --check` CI drift gate), release idempotency +
    94	  release-notes template. Fixes the two latent v1.0.x release.yml bugs
    95	  (RC-version-mismatch; hardcoded release notes).
    96	
    97	### Changed
    98	- `/ceo-boot` extended with liveness checks (fail-open rail silence is
    99	  now surfaced, not mistaken for health) and the harness-config gate.
   100	- README / plugin description / manifests: counts reconciled to disk
   101	  truth (166 skills, 55 hook scripts, 68 `_lib` modules, 26 commands,
   102	  177 ADRs).
   103	
   104	## [1.0.1] - 2026-07-02
   105	
   106	v1.0.1 hardening sweep (PLAN-152) — remediation of the 2026-07-01 post-release
   107	audit fan-out (run `wf_071ef6c5`: 41 confirmed findings) + v1.0.1 backlog.
   108	No new features; security fixes, CI truth, tarball hygiene, model modernization.
   109	
   110	### Security (P0 — shipped-broken in v1.0.0)
   111	- **check_pair_rail PreToolUse gate was FAIL-OPEN since v1.0.0** — the
   112	  settings.json registration passed a relative path the shim could not
   113	  resolve (`hook not found` + `{}` allow). Fixed to the basename +
   114	  `"$CLAUDE_PROJECT_DIR"` form used by the other 43 registrations
   115	  (governance-01).

     1	#!/usr/bin/env bash
     2	# install-npm.sh — local NPM tarball build + smoke-test for ceo-orchestration.
     3	#
     4	# Sprint 13 Phase 2 (PLAN-013) / ROADMAP-CLOSURE Marco 1 — does NOT
     5	# publish. Builds a local tarball + optionally tests it in a temp
     6	# directory. Use this to validate the npm shim before any tag-push
     7	# triggers the real publish workflow (.github/workflows/npm-publish.yml).
     8	#
     9	# Usage:
    10	#   bash scripts/install-npm.sh                   # build tarball only
    11	#   bash scripts/install-npm.sh --smoke           # build + smoke-test in /tmp
    12	#   bash scripts/install-npm.sh --smoke --keep    # smoke + leave artifacts
    13	#
    14	# Exit codes:
    15	#   0 — tarball built (and optional smoke passed)
    16	#   1 — build error
    17	#   2 — smoke-test failure
    18	#   3 — environment missing (node / npm / bash)
    19	#
    20	# Stays disabled for actual publish. The CI workflow npm-publish.yml is
    21	# the only path to npmjs.org and gates through manual approval in the
    22	# production-npm environment (auth = npm Trusted Publishing / OIDC since
    23	# v1.1.0, PLAN-158 Wave 1 — no long-lived token; --provenance is Sigstore
    24	# attestation fed by the same per-run JWT).
    25	
    26	set -euo pipefail
    27	
    28	# -------------------------------- args ---------------------------------------
    29	SMOKE=0
    30	KEEP=0
    31	for arg in "$@"; do
    32	  case "$arg" in
    33	    --smoke) SMOKE=1 ;;
    34	    --keep)  KEEP=1 ;;
    35	    -h|--help)
    36	      cat <<'HELP'
    37	Usage:
    38	  bash scripts/install-npm.sh                   Build local ceo-orchestration tarball only.
    39	  bash scripts/install-npm.sh --smoke           Build + smoke-test the tarball in a /tmp dir.
    40	  bash scripts/install-npm.sh --smoke --keep    Smoke-test and KEEP the temp artifacts for inspection.
    41	
    42	Flags:
    43	  --smoke           Run the smoke-test harness against the freshly built tarball.
    44	                    Creates a throwaway $TMPDIR install + validates that `npx ceo-orchestration`
    45	                    bootstraps a minimal target. Exits 2 on smoke failure.
    46	  --keep            Used with --smoke; preserves the temp install dir for forensic inspection.
    47	                    Without this flag the temp dir is removed on smoke completion.
    48	  -h, --help        Show this help and exit 0.
    49	
    50	Exit codes:
    51	  0 — tarball built (and optional smoke passed)
    52	  1 — build error or unknown arg
    53	  2 — smoke-test failure
    54	  3 — environment missing (node / npm / bash)
    55	
    56	Notes:
    57	  This script DOES NOT publish to the npm registry. It only builds the local tarball
    58	  + optionally validates it locally. Real publishing flows through:
    59	      .github/workflows/npm-publish.yml
    60	  which gates on manual approval in the production-npm environment (npm
    61	  Trusted Publishing / OIDC auth + Sigstore --provenance).
    62	
    63	  Use this to validate the npm shim BEFORE any tag-push triggers the real publish
    64	  workflow. The CI workflow expects this script to have been run on the release
    65	  candidate; manual local validation is the source of truth for the smoke harness.
    66	HELP
    67	      exit 0
    68	      ;;
    69	    *)
    70	      echo "::error::unknown arg: $arg" >&2
    71	      exit 1
    72	      ;;
    73	  esac
    74	done
    75	
    76	# -------------------------------- env check ----------------------------------
    77	for cmd in node npm bash rsync; do
    78	  if ! command -v "$cmd" >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    79	    echo "::error::required command missing: $cmd" >&2
    80	    exit 3
    81	  fi
    82	done
    83	
    84	ROOT="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")/.." && pwd)"
    85	NPM_DIR="$ROOT/npm"
    86	
    87	if [[ ! -d "$NPM_DIR" ]]; then
    88	  echo "::error::npm/ directory missing at $NPM_DIR" >&2
    89	  exit 1
    90	fi

SPEC/v1/audit-log.schema.md:558:| v2.46 | PLAN-135-FOLLOWUP-2 (S234) — no new action, no new fields, `event_schema` stays `v2`, `_KNOWN_ACTIONS` unchanged. **HMAC-integrity fix:** the `statusline_sidecar_write` (o4) percentage fields `context_pct` / `buckets_used_pct_max` are RENAMED to `context_pct_bps` / `buckets_used_pct_max_bps` and re-typed `float`->**integer basis-points** (pct*100), mirroring `fpr_observed_bps`/`pass_rate_bps`/`confidence_bps`. RATIONALE: the canonical encoder (`_lib/canonical_json._validate_no_floats`) forbids any float in an HMAC-covered payload (S181 / ADR-055-AMEND-2); the float form failed `sha compute` on EVERY emit since v2.44 and was written with `hmac=null` + `hmac_error` (and a breadcrumb to `audit-log.errors`) — present in the jsonl but EXCLUDED from the verifiable chain (the action had never once entered the signed chain). **Ranges DIFFER (Sec MF-3 input contract):** `context_pct_bps` 0..10000 (source 0..100%); `buckets_used_pct_max_bps` 0..99900 (source `used_pct` capped at 999% upstream — NO 100% ceiling, so an over-quota burst is not silently floored). The PRODUCER (`.claude/scripts/statusline-ceo.py`, NOT canonical-guarded) owns the `*100` pct->bps scaling and emits finished `_bps` ints; the `_STATUSLINE_SIDECAR_WRITE_ALLOWLIST` scrub branch is the authoritative boundary that int-coerces + clamps (catching `OverflowError` for `float('inf')`) but does NOT re-scale — a direct/future caller is contracted to pass basis-points, not a raw percentage. MIGRATION: zero legacy — no float datum ever entered the verifiable chain and no consumer reads the field (the only reader, `measure_multiplier.py`, reads the separate non-HMAC `statusline-sidecar/v1` JSON FILE, which keeps its float `context_pct` and is NOT renamed). Regression coverage added: every W5 scrub action's emitted event is carried through `canonical_json.encode` and asserted HMAC-encodable — the test gap that hid the born-broken action. | *(field rename + re-type on `statusline_sidecar_write`: `context_pct`->`context_pct_bps` int 0..10000, `buckets_used_pct_max`->`buckets_used_pct_max_bps` int 0..99900; `_STATUSLINE_SIDECAR_WRITE_ALLOWLIST` updated; NO new action — `_KNOWN_ACTIONS` unchanged)* |

+# Sprint 5 Phase 4; registry auth migrated to npm **Trusted Publishing**
+# (OIDC) by PLAN-158 Wave 1 (PLAN-152 §Deferred backlog-oidc successor).
+# Publishes ceo-orchestration on tag push (`v*`): the npm CLI (>=11.5.1,
+# upgraded in-job — Node 20 bundles npm 10.x, which cannot do the
+# exchange) detects the GitHub Actions OIDC context (`id-token: write`)

+# scoped to this repo + workflow + `production-npm` environment as

+# solely as the rollback path:

+        # PLAN-158 W1 (debate, all 3 critics): Node 20 bundles npm 10.x,

       - name: Verify VERSION matches tag
         run: |
           set -euo pipefail
           TAG="${GITHUB_REF_NAME}"
           VERSION_FILE="$(tr -d '[:space:]' < VERSION)"
           EXPECTED="${TAG#v}"
           if [[ "$VERSION_FILE" != "$EXPECTED" ]]; then
             echo "::error::VERSION ($VERSION_FILE) does not match tag ($TAG → $EXPECTED)"

       - name: Populate install.sh self-SHA trailer (P0-15, PLAN-045)
         # PLAN-045 F-15R2-01 / Session 41: install.sh ships with a
         # `# CEO-INSTALL-SHA256: PLACEHOLDER_RELEASE_FILL` trailer as its
         # last line. At publish time, compute sha256 of the script body
         # (all lines EXCEPT the last) and substitute the placeholder with
         # the real hex. The script's own self-verify logic reads the same
         # last-line pattern, so downstream adopters running
         # `bash install.sh ...` trigger a rc=5 fail-CLOSED if the script
         # is modified in transit.
         working-directory: npm
         run: |
           set -euo pipefail
           FILE="scripts/install.sh"
           TRAILER_LINE="$(tail -n 1 "$FILE")"
           if [ "$TRAILER_LINE" != "# CEO-INSTALL-SHA256: PLACEHOLDER_RELEASE_FILL" ]; then
             echo "::error::$FILE trailer not at expected placeholder state"
             echo "got: $TRAILER_LINE"
             exit 1
           fi
           # Compute sha of everything EXCEPT the last line.
           HASH=$(awk 'NR==FNR{n++; next} FNR < n' "$FILE" "$FILE" | sha256sum | awk '{print $1}')
           # In-place substitute ONLY the last line.
           awk -v hash="$HASH" '
             NR == FNR { total = NR; next }
             FNR == total { print "# CEO-INSTALL-SHA256: " hash; next }
             { print }
           ' "$FILE" "$FILE" > "$FILE.new"
           mv "$FILE.new" "$FILE"
           chmod +x "$FILE"
           # Smoke-verify: execute the self-verify branch by running
           # the script without args (hits _verify_self_sha, then usage).
           bash "$FILE" 2>&1 | head -3 || true
           echo "OK: install.sh trailer populated with sha256 $HASH"

+      # guard. Before publishing, ask the registry whether this exact

       # -----------------------------------------------------------------
       # F5 — RC-hold / staleness waiver SUNSET assertion.
       #
       # The pre-GA waivers in .claude/governance/governance-waivers.yaml
       # are honest ONLY while the project is pre-GA (adopter_count=0).
       # Every existing rc_hold/workflow_staleness entry is a 1.x version
       # carrying "Pre-GA ... adopter_count=0". To stop that 100%-waiver
       # escape from silently following the project into GA, this step
       # FAILS the release the moment any waiver `version` parses >= the
       # configured FIRST_GA floor. The floor is the first version at which
       # the framework intends to claim GA / publish to adopters; per
       # ADR-073 the next major (v2.0.0) is the documented GA/breaking
       # boundary, so 2.0.0 is the mechanical sunset. After the first real
       # adopter ships, lower FIRST_GA (or empty the waiver lists) so the
       # ADR-007 RC-hold + 14-day staleness gates resume real enforcement.
       #
       # Today (max waiver 1.0.0 < 2.0.0) this passes; it is a tripwire,
       # not a behavior change for the current pre-GA train.
       #
       # `-rc.N` pre-release suffixes are stripped before comparison: RC
       # tags forensically short-circuit the hold gate (see below), so an
       # rc.* waiver is never an enforcement bypass on its own.
       # -----------------------------------------------------------------
       - name: Assert no waiver has reached the GA sunset floor
         env:
           # First version at which pre-GA waivers are no longer honest.
           # Bump DOWN (or empty the waiver lists) once an adopter ships.
           FIRST_GA: "2.0.0"
         run: |
           set -euo pipefail
           WAIVER_FILE=".claude/governance/governance-waivers.yaml"
           if [[ ! -f "$WAIVER_FILE" ]]; then
             echo "OK: no waiver file present — nothing to sunset"
             exit 0
           fi
 
           # Extract every `version:` value from BOTH waiver sections using
           # the same flag-based section parser the file documents (a range
           # pattern collapses because the start/end regex overlap), strip
           # any -rc.* suffix, then sort -V -u. Iterated via a while-read
           # loop (portable: no mapfile / bash-4 dependency).
           FAILED=0
           COUNT=0
           while IFS= read -r v; do
             [[ -z "$v" ]] && continue
             COUNT=$((COUNT + 1))
             # v >= FIRST_GA  <=>  the smaller of {v, FIRST_GA} under
             # version-sort is FIRST_GA. (Equal floor counts as reached.)
             LOWER="$(printf '%s\n%s\n' "$v" "$FIRST_GA" | sort -V | head -1)"
             if [[ "$v" == "$FIRST_GA" || "$LOWER" == "$FIRST_GA" ]]; then
               echo "::error::Waiver version $v has reached the GA sunset floor (FIRST_GA=$FIRST_GA)"
               echo "::error::Pre-GA RC-hold/staleness waivers are dishonest at or past GA."
               echo "::error::Remove the $v waiver entry (and resume ADR-007 enforcement) or lower FIRST_GA only with a real adopter."
               FAILED=1
             fi
           done < <(
             {
               awk '/^rc_hold:/{f=1; next} f && /^[a-z_]+:/{f=0} f' "$WAIVER_FILE"
               awk '/^workflow_staleness:/{f=1; next} f && /^[a-z_]+:/{f=0} f' "$WAIVER_FILE"
             } \
               | grep -oE '^[[:space:]]*-[[:space:]]*version:[[:space:]]*[0-9][0-9A-Za-z.+-]*' \
               | grep -oE '[0-9][0-9A-Za-z.+-]*$' \
               | sed -E 's/-rc\.[0-9.]+$//' \
               | sort -V -u
           )
 
           if [[ "$COUNT" -eq 0 ]]; then
             echo "OK: waiver file has no version entries to sunset"
             exit 0
           fi
           if [[ "$FAILED" -ne 0 ]]; then
             exit 1
           fi
           echo "OK: all $COUNT waiver versions are pre-GA (< FIRST_GA=$FIRST_GA)"

       # Rule: a GA tag `v1.x.y` MAY only ship after its corresponding
       # RC tag `v1.x.y-rc.N` has existed for ≥24 hours. The 24h window
       # is mechanical: bounds the maximum Codex external re-pass
       # turnaround (anti same-LLM bias per ADR-095 §gate-#6). NOT a
       # "settle period" — vibecoder-only thesis (ADR-096) means no
       # external adopter pressure for calendar buffers.
       #
       # Mechanism:
       #   1. If tag contains `-rc.` → skip check (RC tags always pass)
       #   2. Else find most recent `v<VERSION>-rc.*` tag (by creator date)
       #   3. If none exists → fail (mandatory RC before GA)
       #   4. Else compute delta; reject if < 24h (86400 seconds)
       # -----------------------------------------------------------------
       - name: Assert 24h Codex re-pass window (GA tags only, waiver-aware)
         run: |
           set -euo pipefail
           TAG="${GITHUB_REF_NAME}"
           VERSION="${TAG#v}"
 
           # RC tags short-circuit — they are always permitted.
           if [[ "$TAG" == *-rc.* ]]; then
             echo "::notice::$TAG is an RC tag — skipping 24h hold check"
             exit 0
           fi
 
           # Pre-GA waiver check (PLAN-051 round-19, ADR-007 amendment).
           # During initial framework development with adopter_count=0,
           # the RC-hold window can be waived per Owner authorization
           # recorded in .claude/governance/rc-hold-waivers.yaml. The
           # waiver is additive: post-first-adopter, the file is expected
           # to be empty and ADR-007 default resumes. Each waiver entry
           # cites Owner directive + round-NN sentinel commit.
           WAIVER_FILE=".claude/governance/governance-waivers.yaml"
           if [[ -f "$WAIVER_FILE" ]]; then
             if awk '/^rc_hold:/{f=1; next} f && /^[a-z_]+:/{f=0} f' "$WAIVER_FILE" | grep -qE "^[[:space:]]*-[[:space:]]*version:[[:space:]]*${VERSION}[[:space:]]*$"; then
               echo "::notice::$TAG has a pre-GA RC-hold waiver in $WAIVER_FILE — skipping hold check"
               exit 0
             fi
           fi
 
           # Find the most-recent RC tag for this version, by creator date.
           # `git tag -l --sort=-creatordate` handles both lightweight and
           # annotated tags uniformly via the dereferenced date.
           LAST_RC=$(git tag -l --sort=-creatordate "v${VERSION}-rc.*" | head -1)
 
           if [[ -z "$LAST_RC" ]]; then
             echo "::error::GA tag $TAG has no prior v${VERSION}-rc.* tag"
             echo "::error::Mandatory RC-hold requires a prior RC tag"
             echo "::error::Cut v${VERSION}-rc.1 first; wait 24h (Codex re-pass turnaround); then cut $TAG"
             exit 1
           fi
 
           # Creator-date gives a unix-epoch timestamp for both
           # annotated (tagger date) and lightweight (committer date) tags.
           RC_TS=$(git tag -l --format='%(creatordate:unix)' "$LAST_RC")
           GA_TS=$(git tag -l --format='%(creatordate:unix)' "$TAG")
 
           if [[ -z "$RC_TS" || -z "$GA_TS" ]]; then
             echo "::error::Could not read creator-date for $LAST_RC or $TAG"
             exit 1
           fi
 
           DELTA=$((GA_TS - RC_TS))
           ONE_DAY=$((1 * 86400))
           HOURS=$((DELTA / 3600))
 
           if [[ "$DELTA" -lt "$ONE_DAY" ]]; then
             echo "::error::GA tag $TAG is only $HOURS hours after $LAST_RC"
             echo "::error::Mandatory 24h Codex re-pass window not met (delta=${DELTA}s < 86400s)"
             echo "::error::Wait $((24 - HOURS)) more hours OR run Codex re-pass synchronously and add waiver"
             exit 1
           fi
 
           echo "OK: $TAG is $HOURS hours after $LAST_RC (≥24h Codex re-pass window per ADR-103)"
 
       - name: Assert CHANGELOG entry exists
         run: |
           set -euo pipefail
           TAG="${GITHUB_REF_NAME}"
           VERSION="${TAG#v}"
+          # PLAN-153 Wave B item 5 (c) — same RC normalization as the
+          # "Assert VERSION matches tag" step above: RC tags never get
+          # their own CHANGELOG section; an RC for X.Y.Z validates
+          # against the GA `## [X.Y.Z]` section (which exists at RC-cut
+          # time because the VERSION bump + CHANGELOG entry land before
+          # the RC is tagged). Without this strip the fixed VERSION gate
+          # would just move the RC red run one step later.
+          VERSION="${VERSION%-rc.[0-9]*}"

       - name: Validate install.sh self-SHA mechanism (P0-15, PLAN-045)
         # PLAN-045 F-15R2-01 / Session 41: end-to-end validation that
         # the install.sh self-SHA verification works. We (a) confirm the
         # placeholder is still present (source checkout state), (b) compute
         # the expected sha, (c) substitute it into a temp copy, (d) run the
         # temp copy — self-verify passes → rc=1 (usage exit, not rc=5).
         run: |

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	# SPEC v1 — npm-shim
     2	
     3	> **Spec version:** 1.1.0 (amended PLAN-158 Wave 1 `backlog-oidc` — §Publishing: registry auth migrated to npm Trusted Publishing (OIDC); documentation-of-mechanism change only, shim contract unchanged)
     4	> **Status:** normative
     5	> **Canonical source:** `npm/bin/ceo-orch-init.js`
     6	
     7	The npm package `ceo-orchestration` is a **pass-through shim** around
     8	`scripts/install.sh`. This file locks the contract so adopters can
     9	rely on uniform behavior between `bash install.sh` and `npx ceo-orchestration`.
    10	
    11	## Pass-through invariants (locked in v1)
    12	
    13	1. **Argument forwarding.** Every `process.argv[2..]` argument is
    14	   forwarded unchanged, in order, to the spawned `bash install.sh`
    15	   process. The shim does **not** add, remove, reorder, or rewrite
    16	   arguments.
    17	2. **Exit code passthrough.** The shim exits with the exact exit code
    18	   of the spawned bash process. If the process is killed by signal,
    19	   the shim exits 1.
    20	3. **Stdio inheritance.** stdin, stdout, and stderr are inherited.
    21	   The user sees install.sh's progress live, not buffered.
    22	4. **`__dirname`-relative install location.** The shim resolves
    23	   `install.sh` as `path.join(__dirname, '..', 'scripts', 'install.sh')`.
    24	   It **never** consults `PATH`, environment variables, or working
    25	   directory for installer location.
    26	5. **Zero runtime dependencies.** `package.json`'s `dependencies`
    27	   field is empty (length === 0). CI asserts this on every PR via
    28	   `.github/workflows/smoke-install.yml`.
    29	
    30	## Bundle contents (locked in v1)
    31	
    32	The published tarball contains exactly:
    33	
    34	- `bin/ceo-orch-init.js` (the shim itself)
    35	- `scripts/` (entire framework script directory, incl. `install.sh`)
    36	- `templates/` (template tree shipped to adopters)
    37	- `.claude/` (skills, hooks, plans schema, commands)
    38	- `SPEC/` (this directory)
    39	- `VERSION`, `LICENSE`, `README.md`, `PROTOCOL.md`
    40	
    41	`.npmignore` excludes:
    42	- `node_modules/`, `.git/`, `.github/`, `*.log`, `.DS_Store`
    43	- All `tests/` directories (adopters don't need them)
    44	- `docs/`, `NOTES.md`
    45	
    46	## Versioning
    47	
    48	The shim's version follows the framework's `VERSION` file 1:1. They
    49	are bumped together. There is no separate semver track for the npm
    50	package; if `VERSION=1.2.3`, the npm package is `1.2.3`.
    51	
    52	## Publishing
    53	
    54	`ceo-orchestration` is published from CI on tag push (`v*`) via
    55	`.github/workflows/npm-publish.yml`. Manual `npm publish` is not
    56	used; tags are the only entry point. RC tags (`-rc.*`) are excluded
    57	at the job level; only GA tags publish.
    58	
    59	Registry authentication is npm **Trusted Publishing** (OIDC): the
    60	per-run GitHub OIDC JWT (`id-token: write`) is exchanged by npm CLI
    61	>=11.5.1 (upgraded in-job — Node 20 bundles npm 10.x) for a
    62	short-lived publish credential scoped to the registered trusted
    63	publisher (repo `Canhada-Labs/ceo-orchestration`, workflow
    64	`npm-publish.yml`, environment `production-npm` — an Owner
    65	web-console registration on npmjs.com), still gated behind the
    66	`production-npm` GitHub environment (manual approval before any
    67	publish step). The same JWT feeds the Sigstore `--provenance`
    68	attestation. No long-lived registry token is used: the former
    69	`NPM_TOKEN` granular token is revoked once the first OIDC GA publish
    70	succeeds (PLAN-158 Wave 1, successor of PLAN-152 §Deferred
    71	`backlog-oidc`; until that proof, a rollback to token auth is
    72	pre-staged at
    73	`.claude/plans/PLAN-158/staged/wave1/rollback-oidc-to-token.patch`).
    74	
    75	The publish workflow:
    76	1. Verifies `npm/package.json` `version` matches `VERSION`.
    77	2. Verifies the bundle includes `scripts/install.sh`.
    78	3. Asserts `dependencies` is empty.
    79	4. Publishes with `--provenance` (npm provenance via Sigstore).
    80	
    81	## Exit codes
    82	
    83	| Code | Meaning |
    84	|---|---|
    85	| 0..N | Whatever `install.sh` returned (passthrough) |
    86	| 1 | Spawn killed by signal (no exit code captured) |
    87	| 2 | `install.sh` missing from bundle (packaging bug, not user error) |
    88	
    89	## Deprecation
    90
